  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_638dfc3e-8be9-48e2-a421-d9e241d0b8af'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer356932539553418906">A friendship between the lost and lonely Caroline, and the unhappy Sebastian, leads to an illicit love that threatens them both.<br/>Caroline Wilson is trapped in a cold and loveless marriage with an older man. When her husband finally wins a long sought-after promotion, Caroline feels she has little choice but to follow him to a new home in San Diego. There she meets Sebastian</span>
  <span id="freeText356932539553418906" style="display:none">A friendship between the lost and lonely Caroline, and the unhappy Sebastian, leads to an illicit love that threatens them both.<br />Caroline Wilson is trapped in a cold and loveless marriage with an older man. When her husband finally wins a long sought-after promotion, Caroline feels she has little choice but to follow him to a new home in San Diego. There she meets Sebastian, a young man of 17. <br />For an all too brief summer, their happiness blooms. <br />But external pressures begin to bear down, not least from the overbearing David, and Sebastian’s parents begin to suspect that their son has a secret. Even Caroline’s new friend, Donna, realises that dark passions exist below the serene surface.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536919307?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536919307" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1733498339673113282"><b>4 stars.****Review completed February 19, 2013</b><br/><br/>Sometimes you have to take a chance on love.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/kissing/tumblr_mh1rkycxnk1rb6prdo1_500_zps2daac57a.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409758ra/802559.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mh1rkycxnk1rb6prdo1_500_zps2daac57a.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>The Education of Sebastian</i> is about a summer of stolen happiness. A summer also filled with love, bliss, hope, fear, and recklessness. But it ended badly.<br/><br/>Caroline is married to a US Navy medical officer who is a lot older than her. She was very young when she met him and he swept her off her feet instantly. After a while, however, she realized that she was in for an uninspiring and unkind life. The sex </span>
  <span id="freeText1733498339673113282" style="display:none"><b>4 stars.****Review completed February 19, 2013</b><br><br>Sometimes you have to take a chance on love.<br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/kissing/tumblr_mh1rkycxnk1rb6prdo1_500_zps2daac57a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409758ra/802559.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mh1rkycxnk1rb6prdo1_500_zps2daac57a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The Education of Sebastian</i> is about a summer of stolen happiness. A summer also filled with love, bliss, hope, fear, and recklessness. But it ended badly.<br><br>Caroline is married to a US Navy medical officer who is a lot older than her. She was very young when she met him and he swept her off her feet instantly. After a while, however, she realized that she was in for an uninspiring and unkind life. The sex was desultory and boring. After two years of marriage, David was transferred to the Naval Medical Center in San Diego and he wanted her to be friends with the wife of his new CO. That's how she met Sebastian for the first time, the son of David's new CO. He was eight years old at that time and Caroline was 21. They talked about children's books and a harmless friendship grew between the two. After a while though, David informed her he'd been assigned to Camp Lejeune in North Carolina and they had to move again. Little Sebastian was devastated.<br><br>Many years later Caroline and David come back to San Diego. Caroline is not quite pleased that she had to move again, because she made friends in North Carolina and she had a job that she liked a lot. And then one sunny day on the beach of San Diego fate…happened again in the form of handsome and young Sebastian Hunter. Sebastian is seventeen years old now.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He could sense the feebleness of my will. His lovely eyes were unclouded, free of all doubt, confident and reassuring. And when he leaned forward pressing his lips lightly against mine, it was a peaceful moment at the heart of a whirling pool of emotions. It was an electric moment, the eye of the storm.<br>I tried to understand the feelings that filled me, making me lighter than air. I felt beautiful for the first time in my life, safe and secure.<br>Loved.<br>Cherished.<br><br>"My gallant knight."<br>"Your anything," he said seriously. "But I want to be your everything."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/gifs/gif_3/tumblr_m1b0zr0VUQ1qe9rxvo1_500_zps2a99e83b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409758ra/802560.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m1b0zr0VUQ1qe9rxvo1_500_zps2a99e83b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He jumped and turned around with a scowl on his face which broke into a huge, sexy smile when he saw me.<br>"I've got to go now," he breathed into the phone, "a beautiful woman is feeling me up."<br>"Is that right?"<br>Hidden by the crowd I ran my hand up the front of his jeans.<br>"Yeah," he said into his cellphone, "I don't know what she wants."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>The marriage between Caroline and her husband is (almost) over.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/gifs/tumblr_lyrdc7tQw51r3s7wso1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409758ra/802561.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lyrdc7tQw51r3s7wso1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>(…)Everything had a price. Every glance, every kiss, every stolen touch. It seemed desperately unfair. I didn't want to live without love. Why should I?<br><br>"Caro, don't you understand how I feel about you? I love you. You're all I want. I want a future with you--I want our lives to be together. I'm not a kid. I've had to grow up fast. I've been taking care of myself for a long time now. And I want to take care of you."<br>"I'm just saying that I'll understand when that changes."<br><br>"(…) Why are you so scared? I mean, forget all that legal bullshit…why do you keep trying to…I don't know, make me change my mind? What do you think I've got here that I wouldn't give up in a heartbeat to be with you? There's nothing to keep me here. I'll go anywhere, do anything to be with you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/gifs/tumblr_lyxce6qRgb1qbma4ko1_500_zps3effb1e2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409758ra/802562.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lyxce6qRgb1qbma4ko1_500_zps3effb1e2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"In just over three months, I'll be 18. I could enlist and a few months later I could be sent to the Middle East. I'll be old enough to fight, to die for my country, but you don't think I'll be old enough to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[marry you?" <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>"You want honesty? Well, answer this: if I was 25 and you were 38, would we still be having this conversation?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/quotes/Bildschirmfoto2013-02-16um173441_zps54ec34f9.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409758i/802563.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-02-16um173441_zps54ec34f9.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even though the age of the hero made for some uncomfortable reading moments, I really enjoyed <i>The Education of Sebastian.</i> Most of the time Sebastian came across as pretty mature for his age. There were moments though where his youthfulness shone through, when he'd been sulking or when an unexpected flush of anger flared up. And let's not forget his impatience as well as gushy love confessions. Although there's no getting around it to point out that the story wouldn't have suffered in any way if the hero had been a couple of years older.<br><br>It's quite obvious that the relationship between Caroline and Sebastian has been stimulated by Caroline's unhappy marriage as well as Sebastian's unkind and awful parents. If you don't find love at home then you have to look for it in another place. Caroline soaked up Sebastian's affection and love like a dried out sponge. Geez, I couldn't believe that she could withstand a man like David for so many years. They'd totally grown apart a long time ago after all. As a matter of fact, he used her as his doormat, treated her like crap, was cold and dogmatic. She was his cook, cleaner and occasional sex toy. I was honestly shocked when they had sex. What was <i>that??</i> Hence, I really think that animals show more emotion during intercourse than David and Caroline.<br><br>Of course I understood that she was naïve when she married him. We all have our dreams, we all want love and happiness but when you realize it's not going to happen--ever--then you have to draw the consequences. You just have to move on. Unfortunately she waited way too long, and isn't it kind of ironic that she realized what she wanted out of life when she met such a very young man? Sebastian brought her back to life, he encouraged her to live her dreams, he showed her how to love even though this kind of love will make plenty of readers uncomfortable, including my humble self. Truth be told, I thought she should have insisted they wait until Sebastian's 18th birthday. After all, it was not that far away (only four months). Anyway, what must be, must be and everything has a price. Life is not always fair and sometimes it will end in a huge disaster. Sadly, they had to pay a high price for their summer of love.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Despite what happened that day, despite what happened later, I can't bring myself to regret the events of that summer, because Sebastian taught me how to love.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>What didn't work for me</b><br>I think the book could have been benefitted from better editing. Also, I have never ever read a book before that provided that many colons…colons..colons…all the time. I took the liberty to drop them when I added the quotes to my review. I just can't look at them anymore. Well, I guess one is still there. :)<br><br>I'm off reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17229636.The_Education_of_Caroline__The_Education_of______2_" title="The Education of Caroline (The Education of..., #2) by Jane Harvey-Berrick" rel="nofollow noopener">The Education of Caroline</a>. Update: I'm 59 % done and it's better than the first book. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"There is nothing to forgive," he said, his voice forceful. "We fell in love. It's not a crime."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>*****************************<br><br><b>I know not every reader will enjoy this book. You might want to check out this review:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/534113111">http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/...</a><br><br>And yet I still think that you should be reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17229636.The_Education_of_Caroline__The_Education_of______2_" title="The Education of Caroline (The Education of..., #2) by Jane Harvey-Berrick" rel="nofollow noopener">The Education of Caroline</a> because it's worth a try and definitely better than book 1. :)</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_507961248" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/507961248" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/507961248?book_show_action=true">Jan 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer507961248" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14531226183588790994"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405381i/789580._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405381i/789581._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> <b> “I love you, Caro. I want to make love to you. I want to make love to you forever.” </b> </i><br/><br/>This book made my heart RACE. <b> It was a captivating story of forbidden love. </b> I’m still recovering from the huge cliffhanger ending and most definitely planning to go straight on to book #2.<br/><br/>I gotta say I was a little hesitant going into this one because of the huge age gap between the hero and heroine. For the record, Sebastian is 17 (4 months shy of 18), and Caroline is 30 and (unhappily) married. I kind of w</span>
  <span id="freeText14531226183588790994" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405381i/789580._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405381i/789581._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> <b> “I love you, Caro. I want to make love to you. I want to make love to you forever.” </b> </i><br><br>This book made my heart RACE. <b> It was a captivating story of forbidden love. </b> I’m still recovering from the huge cliffhanger ending and most definitely planning to go straight on to book #2.<br><br>I gotta say I was a little hesitant going into this one because of the huge age gap between the hero and heroine. For the record, Sebastian is 17 (4 months shy of 18), and Caroline is 30 and (unhappily) married. I kind of wavered back and forth a fair bit on it before deciding I should really just give it a shot and I pretty much just jumped in with both feet knowing nothing other than the fact that this one ends on a cliffhanger, but the sequel has a happy ending.<br><br>I want to say that the age difference was totally ‘fine’ but in truth it was almost fine. There were definitely moments where you really felt Seb’s age shine through but then definitely moments where you felt his maturity. There was no doubt though that they were definitely soul-mates, or “right” for each other. It was just their situation that was unfortunate.<br><br><b> I knew from very early on that Seb and Caro would be one of *those* couples I would just want to pluck out of their setting and put them on some desert island somewhere to live out their happy, peaceful, non-judged lives together. But.. *sigh* … that wasn’t going to happen. </b><br><br>There are a few things that made me more okay with the scenario. First, it is <u> NOT </u> a love triangle book. There is no actual wavering back and forth between two guys ever. Caroline is stuck in a loveless marriage to a military man 11 years her senior who she rashly married when she was 19 years old to escape being under her mother’s stifling thumb at home. There is no doubt from the start to the end of the book – she is NOT in love with both men. She is more just ‘stuck’ with her husband. He wasn’t a cruel man, but he was intolerable and insufferable and while he wasn’t directly abusive, the way he treated her was appalling to me and as such, I didn’t lose a moment’s worry over his feelings in the whole matter.<br><br><i> “He hated the way I dressed, the way I spoke, what I spoke about and the things that interested me to speak about… He wasn’t always an unkind man… we were just fundamentally unsuited to each other.” </i><br><br>The story follows Caroline – married to her husband who’s job as a medical officer in the military moved him around a lot. In the prologue, we see them move to a new base where she is introduced to the horrid wife of his new CO and their adorable eight-year-old son Sebastian. She feels badly for him growing up with such wretched parents and the become friends. Its beautiful and totally not creepy guys!! But when her husband is relocated yet again, she is suddenly forced to move again, leaving behind a distraught Sebastian.<br><br>Fast forward 9 years to the present day, Caroline is now 30 and they are moved back to that old base which is where she meets Sebastian Hunter – gorgeous, grown up, and carrying a serious torch for her. He’s truly loved her from since he was a kid and although she resists his advances at first, there is something between them… a spark. A spark she tries to ignore, but ultimately can’t.<br><br><i> “Sebastian, don’t let me keep you from your friends; I’m quite happy to sit here and watch.”<br>He shook his head and looked at me intently.<br>“I can surf anytime; I’d rather be here with you.”<br>I stared down at my notepad, unsure what to say, but absolutely certain that if I looked up I’d be caught in the net of his blue-green gaze. But I also needed to be clear.<br>“I wish you wouldn’t say things like that, Sebastian. I’m a married woman. It makes me… uncomfortable.”<br>I still hadn’t been able to look up….<br>“I really like you, Caroline,” he said softly.<br>I felt his hand touch my arm; he was trembling.<br>I had to look up. His face held such an expression of longing, mixed with anxiety… </i><br><br>Doing the math, she calculates that he must be 18 years old and they begin a relationship in secret at first. But only later does she find out that he is almost 18. Almost. Ohhh what a difference that one tiny word can make. Its terrifying and neither of them went into it knowingly but they are already too deep to pull back and so, despite trying to resist, they can’t help but continue to develop their relationship.<br><br><i> <b> “I knew it was wrong: I knew it was right.”<br><br>“I had chosen – willingly, knowingly, deliberately. I chose love over law. And I didn’t care.” </b></i> <br><br>Its a situation where Caro genuinely did NOT consider him a love interest at first. But he was into her. Like, seriously! And although she struggles at first with her feelings, the heart wants what the heart wants….<br><br><i> “Please don’t,” I whispered. Bu there was no force behind my words.<br>He stood, still holding my hand.<br>“I love you, Caroline.”<br>He spoke softly, but the words were clear, spoken without expectation and with a little hope.<br><br>“I’m married, Sebastian.” …<br>“You don’t love him, Caro.”<br>My eyes darted to his. How did he know? <br>“I love you. I’ll… I’ll do anything, go anywhere … We’ll be happy.”<br>So, so tempting. </i><br><br><i> <b> “We can be together,” he whispered. “Forever.” </b></i>  <br><br>But every single thing between them is forbidden. Its dangerous and there is this HUGE, intense, never-ending undercurrent of pure angst that over-shadows every single one of their interactions.<br><br><i> “Everything had a price: every glance, every kiss, every stolen touch. It seemed desperately unfair…” </i><br><br>I have to say, I pretty much fell in love with Sebastian from the first time he said hi to her on the beach. He was just SUCH a sweet, kind hearted guy. Just one of those guys that you can’t help but crush over – a totally gorgeous character, inside and out. My heart broke for his home life and he did seem a lot more mature than his years at times.<br><br>The writing style is captivating and had a beautiful feeling that just wrapped you into the story.<br><br>This book definitely had that 5-star spark. You know the one I’m talking about, right? The one that makes your heart flutter and have you completely involved in the story.<br><br>The author really made you <b> FEEL </b> all the things they went through – the jealousy and possessiveness, the worries and uncertainty, and their undeniable and passionate feelings for each other.<br><br>But there were also a few things that kept me from being able to give it a full 5 star rating. I didn’t like how much Caro let herself be under her husband’s thumb. I mean, it made sense for the story because if her marriage was solid, it would have thrown the story into a whole different ballpark but I just didn’t like how much of a doormat she was with him. Literally, he said jump, she asked how high. Although, in her defense, she did have a moment toward the end when she finally stood up to him that made me happy.<br><br>And I’m trying how to decide about the age gap. I have mixed feeling about it. First and most importantly, I acknowledge that <u> they were right for each other </u>. Okay, I said it. It was clear they were in love – you felt it, you knew it, it was undeniable. But…. I will say that there were times, as a reader, where it felt a little awkward – I don’t know, moments where his teenager-ness really came through that made me just squint my eyes a little and feel a little uncomfortable. It wasn’t the fact that he was young I had issue with but something about certain scenes made their age gap feel a lot more pronounced. And, I mean, I guess its an honest reaction because the fact of the matter is that it projects their feelings onto you – I mean, Caro had those feelings and went through a lot of anxiety over whether or not they should be together given their age gap so I guess it was really just drawing you into that feeling.<br><br>But yeah, there were definitely moments of “awkward” although kudos to the author for really making you ‘feel’ his age accurately. She didn’t try and dress him up as a man in a kids body. He simple was. a. teenager. A mature one. One who knew, without a doubt what he wanted, who he loved and where he wanted his life to go. This wasn’t one of those “perfect” situations where he’s young but its okay cuz he’s really a man. No. He’s really 17. He had a heart of gold. Was in love for absolute real. But, he was a teen. And she was 30. No sugarcoating it.<br><br>A few of you were asking me about this, so this book is definitely <u> ‘adult‘ </u> in terms of steam. There is a lot of sex and its fairly detailed so definitely not ‘glossed’ over.<br><br>I have to say though that I READ IN FEAR!!!! Seriously, I was freaked WAY the hell out at EVERY moment that they were going to get caught!! I mean, yes, they were careful (to a certain extent) but at the same time they were also just freaking LUCKY they weren’t caught earlier because they did a LOT of things that could have EASILY drawn attention had the wrong person been there at the right time. They really weren’t careful enough for my liking about hiding it so, as cute as they were, I spent half my time freaking out and it did detract a little from my connection because I was SO worried all the time.<br><br><b> <i> “I want to walk on the beach with you and hold your hand and to not be afraid that someone will see us.” </i> </b><br><br>Seriously, the hiding it, having to pretends in public that they weren’t ‘together’, all the stolen glances and fleeting touches, the HUGE looming threat of what would happen if they got caught – EVERYTHING just seriously had my heart in my throat and kept me on pins and needles for a good part of the book. I even had to put the book down a few times and go begging to people for reassurance, lol (yes, I’m a chicken, don’t judge me!!).<br><br>Especially as I got closer to the end and I KNEW there was this giant brutal cliffhanger, I. Couldn’t. Take. It. As it got closer to the end I was freaking out more and more. It was helpless feeling where I knew it was going to end badly and there was absolutely NOTHING I COULD FREAKING DO ABOUT IT!!!!!!!!! I just had to keep reading. And dreading what was to come. And just seriously… F U C K !!!!<br><br>I didn’t cry at the end but my heart was in knots!!!<br><br>I feel utterly wrapped up in Seb and Caro’s story and good or bad, there is no WAY I’m stopping now! So I am absolutely going straight on to book #2 which I have been assured has a HEA!! Thank GOD!! cuz…<br><br><b> <i> “You are my world, Caro,” he said.<br>“And you’re mine.” </i></b> <br><br>*heart clench*<br><br><b> FOR THOSE OF YOU WHO HAVE READ THE BOOK, there is a bonus scene from Seb's POB of his first time with Caro here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/the-education-of-sebastian-bonus-scene-first-time/">http://aestasbookblog.com/the-educati...</a><br><br>My casting images (also above)<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396387i/764026._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405381i/789582.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> Review requested by author. </i> <br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></b></span>

<div id="review_524283149" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/524283149" />
    <a title="Marina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13500406-marina"><img alt="Marina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1361224250p2/13500406.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

Do it for me.”<br>“I’ll always love you, Caro. Don’t give up on us. Please don’t give up. I’ll wait for you. It’s only three years. I love you!”<br>But it wasn’t just three years, was it? I knew that now.<br>“I love you, too,” I whispered so softly I didn’t know if he’d heard me. “Ti amo tanto, Sebastian, sempre e per sempre.”<br>I tried to peel his hands away from my body but he wouldn’t let go.<br>“No!” he cried over and over again. “No!”</b>

<div id="review_512815418" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/512815418" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/512815418?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=steamy-reads">steamy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=emotional-reads">emotional-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=super-romantic-reads">super-romantic-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=need-it-in-paperback">need-it-in-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=freebies">freebies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=amazing-sexual-tension">amazing-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=age-gap">age-gap</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer512815418" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12584959934544629161"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406110i/791880._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406110i/791881._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Wow!!! I absolutely completely utterly totally loved this. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Rules are for the obedience of fools and the guidance of wise men.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>You'll need to excuse me, as I'm precariously hanging in limbo right now, after reading an excrutiatingly painful cliffhanger. But never fear... I have <i>The Education of Caroline</i> patiently waiting for me on my Kindle, to be devoured just as soon as I get through this review... so I must be quick.<br/><br/>I get given plenty of books to review. I love doing it. Some are, i</span>
  <span id="freeText12584959934544629161" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406110i/791880._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406110i/791881._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow!!! I absolutely completely utterly totally loved this. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Rules are for the obedience of fools and the guidance of wise men.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>You'll need to excuse me, as I'm precariously hanging in limbo right now, after reading an excrutiatingly painful cliffhanger. But never fear... I have <i>The Education of Caroline</i> patiently waiting for me on my Kindle, to be devoured just as soon as I get through this review... so I must be quick.<br><br>I get given plenty of books to review. I love doing it. Some are, inevitably, better than others, but I always try and give a fair and accurate review, keeping my responsibility to my blog readers and their tastes in mind. <br><br>Sometimes, I read a book that makes me totally forget I am supposed to be reviewing it and sucks me in entirely. <i>The Education of Sebastian</i> is one such book! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's always been you, Caro. The first time I saw you, I thought you were the most beautiful girl that I'd ever seen. I thought you must be a princess like Cinderella. It's only ever been you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Oh my goodness!! At first, I will admit, I kind of wasn't totally on board with Sebastian and Caroline... I liked them both, I wanted them both to be happy and I could see that they both needed an out from their current lives... but I was convinced that they should be together. Afterall, it was illegal and Sebastian <i>is</i> a child... what does he know about love?!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"What do you think I've got here that I wouldn't give up in a heartbeat to be with you? There's nothing to keep me here: I'll go anywhere, do anything to be with you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>But by the end, I realised how wrong I was! I adored Sebastian! And I was sold on his love for Caroline! He loved her wholly. And she loved him back.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I chose love over law. And I didn't care.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm not going to give too much away, because I wouldn't want to diminish the reading experience for anyone, it's fantastic. All I will say is that the ending ripped my heart out and I'm so hoping <i>The Education of Caroline</i> will restore it to it's rightful place.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Contemplating leaving everything I had ever known of one ill-advised hour of passionate lunacy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This book is steamy, emotional, heart wrenching, thought provoking, soul searching, a little bit naughty and a whole heap of guilty pleasure! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The matter, Sebastian, is that you're a minor. What we've just done... what <i>I've</i> just done... it's against the law. It's a felony, for God's sake!"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>It has notes of <i>On The Island</i> but with it's own scrummy twists and turns thrown in to scramble your poor little mind and get your pulse racing.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Sebastian, women like sex just as much as men... if it's good."<br>He tried to smile but still looked uncertain, his forehead creasing with worry.<br>"Am I...?"<br>He bit his lip.<br>I knew what he was trying to ask me.<br>"Yes, you're good. In fact I'd say you're amazing: in so many ways."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406110ra/791882.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm praying that the delicious Sebastian gets his Caroline and that together they find the happiness they deserve. They're such gorgeous characters and I have a feeling that their story is about to get even more exciting. I can't wait, so, if you'll excuse me, I'm off to find out...<br><br>Read this book! It's fab and it deserves for more people to be talking about it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406110i/791883._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12584959934544629161" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag"><img alt="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410910791p2/8191340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/523325402?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=cliffy">cliffy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=male-virgin">male-virgin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=waiting">waiting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=underage-love">underage-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523325402" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15232746195216180892"><blockquote>
  <b>“You’ve brought me to life – and you’ll never know how much I owe you because of that.”</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407680i/796559.png' width='3500' height='250"' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I know I am going to sound a bit like a broken record as many people have judged this book without reading it and I to had an opinion before reading it. As a Mother of a 17-year-old son, I thought-ugh no way this can work but then I remembered going into On The Island with much hesitation and completely loving the book. So… I began the story of Caroline and Sebastian: a truly enthralling story of forbidden</span>
  <span id="freeText15232746195216180892" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>“You’ve brought me to life – and you’ll never know how much I owe you because of that.”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407680i/796559.png" width="3500" height='250"' alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know I am going to sound a bit like a broken record as many people have judged this book without reading it and I to had an opinion before reading it. As a Mother of a 17-year-old son, I thought-ugh no way this can work but then I remembered going into On The Island with much hesitation and completely loving the book. So… I began the story of Caroline and Sebastian: a truly enthralling story of forbidden love.<br><br>Both Caroline and Sebastian were alone in their home life; Caroline rejected by her Mother and now in a loveless marriage. Sebastian, at the age of 8 is emotionally and physically abused by his parents and practically raising himself. He finds a friend, teacher and someone that truly cares about him in Caroline and forms a loving bond with her, one that he held on to. <br><br>When she reappears in his life almost ten years later, he has not forgotten her and now is in love with her. <br>This is where the story takes the reader on a journey of two souls that are so right for one another, but in the eyes of society are so wrong. <br><blockquote>
  <b>“It’s always been you, Caro. The first time I saw you, I thought you were the most beautiful girl that I’d ever seen."</b>
</blockquote><br>The author describes the development of Seb and Caro’s forbidden relationship in such relatable detail that I felt every emotion of a 17-year-old young man as well as a 30-year-old women. <br>The discovery and awakening of their love was written so beautifully and the way the author wrote the voice of the H/h, with their uncertainty, jealously, possessiveness and deep passion for one another seemed so real and authentic.<br> I felt like I was with them on the beach, in the car, in their bedrooms, in the storeroom and in the bathroom. <br>Sebastian’s sweet innocence was heart warming, but in all of his inexperience he was still man enough to be a quick and aggressive learner.<br><br>Of course all good things come to an end and this forbidden love was discovered and things did not end well…. Or did they?<br><br>You, the reader will need to read this wonderful story and find out …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407680i/796560.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I love you, Sebastian. So much, tesoro.” And then I walked away, leaving behind all the goodness and beauty that I’d ever known in my life.”</b>
</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15232746195216180892" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_642836613" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/642836613" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820197-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383385041p2/3820197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/642836613?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer642836613" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8185982720807550510"><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425591i/849509.jpg' width='350' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425591i/849510.jpg' width='350' height='440' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/>There are already a million reviews out there (and about two million gifs....make that two million...and <i>two</i>!) of this book. So, for the other three people who haven't read this yet and who may be considering it, here are a few of my thoughts on <b>
  <i>The Education of Sebastian.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Married at nineteen to a man eleven years older, a medical officer in the US Navy, Caroline Wilson feels isolated as a military wife. She's unsophisticated, uneducated and young. At twenty-one, she meets and befriends Se</span>
  <span id="freeText8185982720807550510" style="display:none"><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425591i/849509.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425591i/849510.jpg" width="350" height="440" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>There are already a million reviews out there (and about two million gifs....make that two million...and <i>two</i>!) of this book. So, for the other three people who haven't read this yet and who may be considering it, here are a few of my thoughts on <b>
  <i>The Education of Sebastian.</i>
</b><br><br>Married at nineteen to a man eleven years older, a medical officer in the US Navy, Caroline Wilson feels isolated as a military wife. She's unsophisticated, uneducated and young. At twenty-one, she meets and befriends Sebastian Hunter, the eight year-old son of another military family. Their friendship is short-lived as often the case within the military community, moving to different bases around the country. They meet again, Caroline is thirty.<br><br><b>The Good</b><br>Jane Harvey-Berrick has a very nice writing style, her prose polished and above average, especially for the contemporary romance genre. The writing in first person from Caroline's pov suits this story well.<br><br>Caroline is a likeable heroine. Sebastian is written I think particularly well as a sweet, caring, yet mature teenager. <br><br>Their relationship is believable, romantic and sweet.<br><br>There is a lot of sex.<br><br><b>The Not-So-Good</b><br>There is a lot of sex. It can and does become a little tiresome, despite it being well-written.<br><br>For those readers who dislike cheating in any way, shape or form, this book will not be for you. Caroline is married, albeit unhappily, but embarks on an affair with Sebastian.<br><br>The plot here is pretty thin. Nothing actually happens. Besides the sex, of course....and their developing relationship. It's very much a slow, character-driven story.<br><br>Caroline is likeable, but a bit of a doormat. I realise she was young when she married, but I wish she'd stood up for herself a bit with her husband. As the adult here she was also reckless and at times clueless.<br><br>This complaint is I realise, redundant now. But the book does end on a cliffie. No waiting, as book #2 has been released. Just have it ready if you're going to continue reading the series.<br><br>Some readers may already know, but <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Sebastian is only seventeen when he and Caroline begin their affair. Under Californian law he is a minor and their sexual relationship is illegal. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Steam:</b> 3-3.5<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8185982720807550510" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_589286309" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/589286309" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/589286309?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=battle-of-the-books-2013">battle-of-the-books-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-a-h">authors-a-h</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=lendable">lendable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer589286309" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer963645349858490946"><blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825806.jpg' alt=' photo images14_zpsb1d924bd.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote><br/><br/>Painful, beautiful and heartrending. This is a beautifully written love story that grabbed my heart and never let go.<br/>I really loved the two characters - Sebastian & Caroline.<br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1304.photobucket.com/user/Alex_Economides/media/characters%20women%202/characters%20women%203/03ff91d25f3d96e1f60aa9d466cdc02e_zpsc343b1f7.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825808._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 03ff91d25f3d96e1f60aa9d466cdc02e_zpsc343b1f7.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><blockquote>
<b><i>He lifted my chin with his fingers to make me look into his eyes.<br/>“There’s nothing to forgive,” he said, his voice forceful. “We fell in love: it’s not a crime.”</i></b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825809.png' alt=' photo xgza3qkgi61r7o9rpk2m_zps3f047b22.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/>The love story between Sebastian and Caroline was totally believable for me. <br/><br/>I have a cousin, who at 18 met and fell in love with a lovely,</span>
  <span id="freeText963645349858490946" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825806.jpg" alt=" photo images14_zpsb1d924bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br><br>Painful, beautiful and heartrending. This is a beautifully written love story that grabbed my heart and never let go.<br>I really loved the two characters - Sebastian &amp; Caroline.<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1304.photobucket.com/user/Alex_Economides/media/characters%20women%202/characters%20women%203/03ff91d25f3d96e1f60aa9d466cdc02e_zpsc343b1f7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825808._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 03ff91d25f3d96e1f60aa9d466cdc02e_zpsc343b1f7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>He lifted my chin with his fingers to make me look into his eyes.<br>“There’s nothing to forgive,” he said, his voice forceful. “We fell in love: it’s not a crime.”</i></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825809.png" alt=" photo xgza3qkgi61r7o9rpk2m_zps3f047b22.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>The love story between Sebastian and Caroline was totally believable for me. <br><br>I have a cousin, who at 18 met and fell in love with a lovely, not happily married woman of 34. Despite the many “it will never work, too much of an age difference” remarks, they did get married after her divorce, had a child and are still happily married and together 26 YEARS!!!!<br><br>I think that if Caroline had just only waited for Sebastian to turn 18, their love story may have not created the pain they both experienced when their relationship was discovered. The choices they both made may not have been right but then I have never been faced with something like they were so it was pretty difficult for me to make any judgments. I just kept hoping that things would not end badly for them. And things did end in such a painful and sad way.<br><br><blockquote><b><i>“I have to go now, tesoro,” I said softly, stroking his neck.<br>His grip tightened around me. “No!” he gasped as if he was in great pain.<br>“Yes. Sebastian, listen to me. I want you to have a good life, tesoro, a big life. I want you to be happy, to fall in love…”<br>“No, God, no, Caro! Don’t say that!”<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417479ra/825810.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mlt7l1t7sg1s3a4y7o1_500_zpsf272fd7b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>“Yes! Do it for me.”<br>“I’ll always love you, Caro. Don’t give up on us. Please don’t give up. I’ll wait for you. It’s only three years. I love you!”<br>But it wasn’t just three years, was it? I knew that now.<br>“I love you, too,” I whispered so softly I didn’t know if he’d heard me. “Ti amo tanto, Sebastian, sempre e per sempre.”</i></b></blockquote><br><br><br>Caroline feels trapped in a loveless marriage and realizes that something is missing in her life, that’s forgotten who she is. She went from a life of being sheltered by her parents to marrying a man who has never shown her any real love and acceptance or recognized the person she was. <br>At times I found her to be somewhat “immature” but there were so many things in her life that she had never experienced and as I got to know her better, I was more understanding about the way she did certain things. Feeling alive, feeling loved and loving. So intoxicating!! <br><br>Their love scenes are beautiful, sensual and breathtaking.<br><br><blockquote><b><i>Sebastian leaned back in his chair and I took a deep breath.<br>“Is it always like this?” he said, suddenly looking lost and vulnerable.<br>I knew what he was asking me and I didn’t have an answer. I shook my head. “Not for me… not until now, until you.”<br>What did I know of the kind of love that made it hard to breathe, where your body ached day and night for that connection with another, physically, mentally, spiritually? It was utterly new and terrifying and exhausting and<br>wonderful. I was dazzled by the light that spilled from him into the shadow of my previous existence. He eclipsed everything, erased everything that had gone before. I was reborn – not just to him, but to myself. And I was ready for the adventure.</i></b></blockquote><br><br>Sebastian’s life has not been easy. Despite the abuse and cruelty by his parents and the lack of any love from them, he’s still able to be a kind, caring and loving person. I fell in love with him from the very beginning. He has such a loving heart, a sweetness in him that pulled at my heartstrings. A longing to love and be loved. To matter to someone. <br>I loved seeing the two sides of him…the young and carefree and the deeper side of him. Almost hard to believe he was so young. He’s so open about his feelings for Caroline, who questions her feelings about their relationship.<br><br><blockquote><b><i>He looked up.<br>“You want honesty? Well, I don’t know what will happen… but neither do you. Maybe we’ll make it… maybe we won’t. But you’re giving up before we’ve even tried. I don’t understand. Why won’t you take a chance?”<br><br>The most incredible feeling of love welled up inside me. I was so lucky. He was kind and thoughtful and caring. He was fun to be with; beautiful inside and out. I didn’t know a lover could be a friend, too. And he loved me.<br>Me.<br>But was I really strong enough to follow my heart and to hell with the consequences? Could I expect a 17 year old boy… man… to be strong enough for this? No, that wasn’t right. I was the one who had to be strong: for both of us.</i></b></blockquote><br><br>The interaction between Caroline and Sebastian is beautiful and intense, totally captivating me.<br><blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825811.jpg" alt=" photo 30c31e8853c5cadda8afa7e5ef82d0cf_zps1498d213.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><a href="http://s1304.photobucket.com/user/Alex_Economides/media/characters%20couples%202/tumblr_mfz85eLxVh1r8ufr0o1_500_zps5d40dd61.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417479ra/825812.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfz85eLxVh1r8ufr0o1_500_zps5d40dd61.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><b><i> Sebastian was singing to himself. I strained to hear the words. When I did, my heart broke open, filling with the love that poured from those faint, heartfelt words. Peace and joy and a sense of wholeness that I’d never known utterly overwhelmed me and I began to cry softly.<br> When I hear her voice, the world disappears<br> When I hear her voice, I have no more fears.<br>I had never believed it was possible to cry from happiness.<br><br>She takes away the sadness, she takes away the pain<br>She takes away the darkness, she takes away the rain.<br>He stretched up to pull down two white towels, placing them carefully at the side of the bath.<br>When I’m traveling from so far away<br>She’s my path, she’s my sun, she lights my way.<br>Then he turned and saw me standing in the shadows.<br>“Caro! Why are you crying?”<br>“Because I love you.”</i></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417479i/825813.jpg" alt=" photo c6267704693b7f33953b720e795cd95f_zps5ca0686b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>Two lonely souls that find something in each other that fills the void in their lives, in their hearts.<br><br><blockquote><b><i>I knew why he thought that, why he would say that, but I couldn’t let him blame himself.<br>“It’s not your fault, Sebastian,” I said gently, stroking his arm. “You’re the one good thing I’ve got in my life. I wouldn’t change that for anything. Not for anything. I finally feel… alive.”<br>I heard him gasp and he pulled me closer.<br>“I feel the same, Caro. You’ve taught me everything I know.”<br>I blinked in surprise.<br>“You have. You’ve taught me who I can be, you’ve made me stronger. You make me want to see the magic in the world. I didn’t know falling in love could be… like this.”<br>Was that really how he felt? Is that how he saw me: someone who could make him stronger? How did that happen? I was so weak and cowardly. But, and I felt a small flowering of hope inside me, I had changed, hadn’t I. I was getting stronger: not yet strong, but getting there.<br>It felt as if he’d been the one to teach me. Perhaps we had learned together.</i></b></blockquote><br><br>By the time I came to the end of the story, I felt heartbroken. Totally devastated. The sadness, the pain – jeez, I could not stop the tears falling .........<br><blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417479ra/825814.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mm1awprgOX1so450so1_250_zps7c3c5778.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>when i read this........I cried buckets!!!<br><blockquote><b><i>Then my eyes rested on the man I loved; the man I vowed I would never see again because he’d been hurt enough – by me.<br>“Caro, no!” he cried again, tears falling down his face, mingling with the blood.<br>“I love you, Sebastian. So much, tesoro.”<br>And then I walked away, leaving behind all the goodness and beauty that I’d ever known in my life.</i></b></blockquote><br><br>I know that there’s a follow-up to their story and I just hope that they will find each other again and be together. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="963645349858490946" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/524437223" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524437223?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524437223" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10017372257816998260"><b>5 Amazing heart shattering stars!!! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/058cac48-dec6-4373-be93-23f825602979_zps42d4a3b5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407846i/797102.jpg' alt=' photo 058cac48-dec6-4373-be93-23f825602979_zps42d4a3b5.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>A beautiful, intense, passionate, devastating, forbidden love story. Loved it!!! I will say, when you finish this one, be ready to jump straight into book 2! <br/><br/>Caroline is in a loveless marriage. At 30 years old, and being married for 11 of those years, she is living a lonely and empty life. Being with David is sucking the life out of her. David is an officer in the Navy. They are living out east, but he gets transferred to California. They move back to San </span>
  <span id="freeText10017372257816998260" style="display:none"><b>5 Amazing heart shattering stars!!! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/058cac48-dec6-4373-be93-23f825602979_zps42d4a3b5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407846i/797102.jpg" alt=" photo 058cac48-dec6-4373-be93-23f825602979_zps42d4a3b5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A beautiful, intense, passionate, devastating, forbidden love story. Loved it!!! I will say, when you finish this one, be ready to jump straight into book 2! <br><br>Caroline is in a loveless marriage. At 30 years old, and being married for 11 of those years, she is living a lonely and empty life. Being with David is sucking the life out of her. David is an officer in the Navy. They are living out east, but he gets transferred to California. They move back to San diego where there were stationed around 9 years ago. Caroline see’s a familiar face when she is out and about. Sebastian. At first she doesn’t recognize him. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/af36cb9d-fd31-4c35-91f6-460c69a5aa98_zps9e545c9a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407846i/797103.jpg" alt=" photo af36cb9d-fd31-4c35-91f6-460c69a5aa98_zps9e545c9a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>When she last saw Seb, he was only 8 years old. He has horrible parents, so he would visit Caroline and her father a lot as a child. He’s not a child anymore. Sebastian is now 17, but he looks much older than that. He recognizes Caroline right away. Oh dear, Sebastian... I love that guy! He does not have the maturity level of a 17 (almost 18) year old. The two of them start to catch up with each other. There is a pretty obvious connection and attraction, though Caroline tries to deny it at first. It’s one of those loves that is once in a life time and completely undeniable. Sebastian brings Caroline back to life.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/d5eca64c-fc12-4f8d-8845-7a08cdef188d_zps366e4128.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407846i/797104.jpg" alt=" photo d5eca64c-fc12-4f8d-8845-7a08cdef188d_zps366e4128.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>I knew it was wrong: I knew it was right.</b><br><br>They are keeping their relationship a secret until he turns 18, then they are going away together. Caroline knows what she’s doing is risky, but their love is worth taking a chance on. <br><br><b>
  <i>“There’s nothing to forgive.” he said, his voice forceful. “We fell in love: it’s not a crime.”<br><br>“I chose love over law. And I didn’t care.” </i>
</b><br><br>They have to get creative spending time together...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e99e3b2c-609a-4bee-953b-0c5343a3f79c_zps04f25bec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407846i/797105.jpg" alt=" photo e99e3b2c-609a-4bee-953b-0c5343a3f79c_zps04f25bec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Not only was this a beautiful story, it was smoking hot! Wow! <br>These two have crazy chemistry.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/GIFS/gif-eos3_zpsb061839c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407846ra/797106.gif" alt=" photo gif-eos3_zpsb061839c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“It’s always been you, Caro.”</i>
</b><br><br>I am so in love with these two. The age difference was really not that big of a thing. Caro isn’t after a younger guy. She just loves Sebastian. And Sebastian is crazy in love with her. He is protective over her, such a sweet guy, and no matter what other women are around, he only sees Caro. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I don’t care about anyone else,” he said fiercely. “Just you.”<br><br>“My gallant knight.” <br>“Your anything,” he said seriously. <br>“But I want to be your everything.”</i>
</b><br><br>Unfortunately, their situation is not ideal. Even when Caro leaves her husband, they can’t openly be together. It is really sad. I am a sucker for forbidden love and messed up/unconventional relationships. I was rooting for these two the whole book. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/8d175fef-27bd-41a4-80a0-298b36a0c936_zps2a806388.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407846i/797107.jpg" alt=" photo 8d175fef-27bd-41a4-80a0-298b36a0c936_zps2a806388.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Would it really matter if they were 20 and 33, or how about 30 and 43... No one would care! How many woman get married in their 20’s to men in their 30’s? I get it... Sebastian was a minor. But he was a high school graduate and so close to 18, I don’t think it counts. <br><br>Now, as beautiful as their love story was, the ending was tragic... The last few pages seriously had me a hot mess!!!<br><br> I was kinda like this...<br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/images/why%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380350291ra/704132.gif" alt="why gifs photo: tumblr_lsxz4nhLyR1r0ty4s.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>then this...<br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/GIFS/gif-eos2_zps05c581e4.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403956ra/785968.gif" alt=" photo gif-eos2_zps05c581e4.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and lastly like this...<br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/GIFS/gif-eos1_zps7d86dbab.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383940ra/742352.gif" alt=" photo gif-eos1_zps7d86dbab.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The ending of this book gutted me. I was an emotional wreck, crying hysterically. I swear, if these two don’t manage to get their happy ever after, I may lose my shit. <br><br>After reading this story- <br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/GIFS/gif-eos4_zps7873b126.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403956ra/785969.gif" alt=" photo gif-eos4_zps7873b126.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>Just a side note: After reading BOTH books in this series, if the age difference is a deal breaker for you , give the second book a shot! The Education of Caroline was a fabulous read! But I would highly recommend both of these two :D </i></span>

<div id="review_536895021" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536895021" />
    <a title="Mo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11856352-mo"><img alt="Mo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371247812p2/11856352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536895021?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536895021" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14645499064266622139">Well, that was a bit of a roller-coaster. Was very wary about starting this. I mean I have a son who is nearly 17 - did I want to go down that road in this book. It had things that I do not like in books, infidelity, underage sex! But I saw the great reviews by a lot of friends and I know their taste is good so went for it. I really liked it. Yes, the age thing did bother me a bit - he is 17, she is 30, he is legally under the age of consent. I know in America it is different ages in different S</span>
  <span id="freeText14645499064266622139" style="display:none">Well, that was a bit of a roller-coaster. Was very wary about starting this. I mean I have a son who is nearly 17 - did I want to go down that road in this book. It had things that I do not like in books, infidelity, underage sex! But I saw the great reviews by a lot of friends and I know their taste is good so went for it. I really liked it. Yes, the age thing did bother me a bit - he is 17, she is 30, he is legally under the age of consent. I know in America it is different ages in different States. But it was a fairly powerful love story. OK, you are thinking, he is only 17, what does he know about love but I really felt he did love Carolina - coming from his background I can see how he might have jumped into any kind of loving relationship but I believe the connection was there long ago. My heart was in my mouth a lot of the time, waiting for them to be caught. Think they took a few too many risks. Was it worth it? Not sure - yes, there was the "cliffhanger" - did I say recently that I was not reading any more of these "cliffhanger" books?? I doubt I would have started it if I did not have the next one to dive into straight away. I thought the writing was very good, the characters portrayed very well, even the non-main characters. Would recommend this book. Hopefully Book 2 will end up the way i want it to end!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14645499064266622139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</a><br/><br/>This is what I've been waiting for, a book about cheating with another man but the other man is not a dick and the husband is a dick. All of the stories I've read or watched that had cheating on it would end in a disaster. Like this new movie coming out called <u>"The Boy Next Door</u> with Jennifer Lopez in it, you could tell that the "boy" is a bad guy and things go to hell. This book was exactly what I've been in a mood for. <br/><br/>Caroline has been together with her husba</span>
  <span id="freeText3659013259086984052" style="display:none"><b>4.5 'Love Knows No Age' Stars</b> <br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpso7ykudff.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
