</a><br><br>This is what I've been waiting for, a book about cheating with another man but the other man is not a dick and the husband is a dick. All of the stories I've read or watched that had cheating on it would end in a disaster. Like this new movie coming out called <u>"The Boy Next Door</u> with Jennifer Lopez in it, you could tell that the "boy" is a bad guy and things go to hell. This book was exactly what I've been in a mood for. <br><br>Caroline has been together with her husband for 11 years. She knows she isn't happy with him. Get this, she is not his <i>wife</i> or partner, she's basically his slave. She's supposed to be the 'perfect' wife. "Yes honey" "I'm sorry honey". She nows that's not her but she doesn't say anything. <br><br>Sebastian is the boy that Caroline used to look after because his shitty-alcoholic parents couldn't. But now that Caroline is back to town and meets Sebastian again he's no longer the 8 year old she ince new, he's now a built-hot-tanned-surfer. You could tell there was a connection when they reunited. Before they started getting "intimate" Caroline didn't know that Sebastian was only 17. That was one of the reasons what they were doing was wrong. <br><br><b>Had I reached a turning point in my life, or was this merely a blip on a long and bleak horizon? Was leaping from a failed relationship to a doomed one the most sensible action for a woman of thirty? Rationally: no. But the feel of Sebastian’s body against mine, inside mine; his sweetness, his gentleness... Could I really say that meant nothing? Were those feelings so abundant in my life that I could count them worthless.</b><br><br>Lets talk about David, he is a reason that makes me want to never wanna get married. There's like a huge amount of men that use their wives as maids than soul mates. He pissed me off badly. That's why she was happy that she cheated on him.<br><br><b>I was crying and laughing and crying. How ridiculous. Of course it wasn’t going to be okay. How ridiculously happy and terrified and happy I felt.</b><br><br>Sebastian made her feel wanted, beautiful, and alive. She've never felt that way with David. She felt <i>loved</i> for the first time. <br><br><b>Fate had thrown us together: who was I to deny it? No, that wasn’t right. I simply no longer cared. I had chosen – willingly, knowingly, deliberately. I chose love over law. And I didn’t care.</b><br><br>This book was simply beautiful. Love doesn't know any age difference. I loved caro and Sebastian. But I couldn't help but fall in love with Sebastian. He might've been 17 but he's mature for his age. <br><br><b>“You’ve taught me who I can be, you’ve made me stronger. You make me want to see the magic in the world. I didn’t know falling in love could be… like this.”</b><br><br>I was praying that the ending wouldn't piss me off, but I guess my prayers weren't answered. Thank the God that there's a second book, if there wasn't I think I would've died a thousand deaths. <br><br>Simply Amazing.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpslhywbczm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422736530i/13540026._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpslhywbczm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“You are my world, Caro,”<br><br>“And you’re mine.”</i>

<span id="freeTextContainer7684876112077487215"><b>Intense ~ Passionate ~ Engaging ~ Riveting ~ Romantic</b> <br/><br/>I began this book with much skepticism due to the underage hero along with the vast differences between his age and that of the heroine. She's thirty, in a loveless marriage and he has a few months before his eighteenth birthday. <br/><br/>I would never have dreamed how much I would enjoy their journey! It's riveting, intense, powerful, passionate and one of my most captivating reads this year! <br/><br/>There are circumstances that have made Sebastian Hunter ma</span>
  <span id="freeText7684876112077487215" style="display:none"><b>Intense ~ Passionate ~ Engaging ~ Riveting ~ Romantic</b> <br /><br />I began this book with much skepticism due to the underage hero along with the vast differences between his age and that of the heroine. She's thirty, in a loveless marriage and he has a few months before his eighteenth birthday. <br /><br />I would never have dreamed how much I would enjoy their journey! It's riveting, intense, powerful, passionate and one of my most captivating reads this year! <br /><br />There are circumstances that have made Sebastian Hunter mature beyond his years. Not only is he incredibly handsome, but very endearing and oh-so-lovable! Carolina Wilson aka Caroline is coasting through life in a loveless marriage, following the orders of her overbearing husband. Now, for the first time in her life her <i>tesoro</i> makes her feel alive. <br /><br />This is a new-to-me author and she has an amazing talent for storytelling. JHB has crafted an engaging, well written story with a cast of complex characters and included a plot that makes it impossible to put down. <br /><br />There is a major cliffhanger at the end. Make sure you have Book #2 on hand! <br /><br /><b> "ti amo tanto, sempre e per sempre" </b><br /><br /><i>Thank you Babs and Ellen for giving me the push to read this series!</i><br /><br /></span>

Book 1 was not for me but I am really happy I decided to read book 2 because is BRILLIANT!!! *** <br><br>If you want to read a GREAT review about book 1, click here:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536919307">http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/...</a> </b><br><br><br>-----------------------------------------------------------------------<br><br><br><b>SORRY buddies but I am not in love with this story, I am leaving this one for a while and will try to finish it tomorrow but it's too sweet for me. Man up bitch! You are waiting 4 months to leave your hubby because you are not able to do it on your own, we are in 2013, get a job doing whatever and manage your life!</b><br><br>And then I found some parts funny and they were NOT meant to be funny!<br><br>*I take it that he is 17 but a <b>box of condoms</b> in a few hours???? I have a good, scratch that, great sexual life and you don't use 12 condoms (or was that a 24 condoms box?) in a few hours. That's the most normal thing ever!<br><br>*Next day, Sebas brings <b>ANOTHER BOX OF CONDOMS</b>, YEAH!!! You and your sweet c*ck are AWESOME! <br><br>*That menopause comment?! <br><br>*Sebas, don't come to see La Alhambra until you are in book 2, ok? We don't like sweet guys and you come with sugar on top!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409339i/801524.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>I will finish this, hell yeah (or I'll try) and then I will read book 2 because I know I am going to love cocky Sebas!</b><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/561960641?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561960641" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7533837213446092534">4 HEART WRENCHING STARS.<br/><br/>I certainly wasn't sure about this book going in to it, but as ever I was tempted by the great reviews and it's popularity on GR.<br/><br/>My heart was literally in my mouth the whole way through this book. Bittersweet love, heartache, forbidden encounters ~ This is the journey of Caroline and Sebastian, An emotional account of two people, who find each other in the midst of their equally saddening circumstances. The book had a way of drawing me in, with it's intrigue and passion i</span>
  <span id="freeText7533837213446092534" style="display:none">4 HEART WRENCHING STARS.<br /><br />I certainly wasn't sure about this book going in to it, but as ever I was tempted by the great reviews and it's popularity on GR.<br /><br />My heart was literally in my mouth the whole way through this book. Bittersweet love, heartache, forbidden encounters ~ This is the journey of Caroline and Sebastian, An emotional account of two people, who find each other in the midst of their equally saddening circumstances. The book had a way of drawing me in, with it's intrigue and passion i I was almost desperate to see how the story would end.<br /><br />Overall I found this difficult to rate, at times I did feel uncomfortable with the content of the story. But their is no doubt that I fell in love with the characters and book two becomes a necessity after completing this story.<br /><br />This book has 5 star ratings almost everywhere, the authors talent of writing a story of taboo proportions, that is gorgeously written and dare I say enjoyable astounded me. I was a nervous wreck most of the way through the story, so that did take away some of the enjoyment level of my reading experience. This is undoubtably a 5 star read but I can only give it 4 overall.<br /><br />A conflicted 4 stars.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1843765277533450573">This is NOT my type of romance. I do NOT usually read books that involve an age difference like this story. <br/><br/>That said, a good friend recommended, so I read.<br/><br/>I LOVED this story. It's more than the sexual relationship. It's about love and maturity. It's about finding that ONE person, despite external forces being NOT in your favor.<br/><br/>My advice: give it a chance. I'm glad I did. </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=waiting-for-next-book-b4-reading">waiting-for-next-book-b4-reading</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525234276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15580173714707941044">4.5-4.75 Stars<br/><br/>*Meet Sebastian & Caroline<br/><a href='http://s1094.beta.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/SebastianinTheEducationofSebastian_zps69cf94d3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407961i/797448.jpg' alt=' photo SebastianinTheEducationofSebastian_zps69cf94d3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>He kissed me with sudden ferocity, covering my face and throat with hard, burning kisses. His weight pinned me down as I ran my hands across the taut muscles of his back and shoulders.<br/>“I love you,” he growled. “That’s all that matters.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>When I came across this book, I wanted to read it like ASAP. The only thing that stopped me was that I knew it ended in a cliffhanger, so I waited for the release of the second book. As soon as book two was released</span>
  <span id="freeText15580173714707941044" style="display:none">4.5-4.75 Stars<br><br>*Meet Sebastian &amp; Caroline<br><a href="http://s1094.beta.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/SebastianinTheEducationofSebastian_zps69cf94d3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407961i/797448.jpg" alt=" photo SebastianinTheEducationofSebastian_zps69cf94d3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>He kissed me with sudden ferocity, covering my face and throat with hard, burning kisses. His weight pinned me down as I ran my hands across the taut muscles of his back and shoulders.<br>“I love you,” he growled. “That’s all that matters.” </i>
</b><br><br>When I came across this book, I wanted to read it like ASAP. The only thing that stopped me was that I knew it ended in a cliffhanger, so I waited for the release of the second book. As soon as book two was released, I was all over it like white on rice. I knew the premise of the story involved a thirty-year-old woman and her 17-year-old lover. Yes, that’s right: <i>Seventeen!</i> Did it bother me? Nope. I LOVED it just the way it is. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You want honesty? Well, I don’t know what will happen… but neither do you. Maybe we’ll make it… maybe we won’t. But you’re giving up before we’ve even tried. I don’t understand. Why won’t you take a chance?” ~Sebastian </i>
</b><br><br>Caroline is thirty and stuck in a loveless marriage. She married David when she was only nineteen years old. Eleven years after, she’s utterly miserable. He constantly mistreats her and takes her for granted. He’s a navel officer and traveling comes second nature. When they return to San Diego for the second time around, this is when her life begins to change. <br><br>She’s known Sebastian since he was eight years old. Now, don’t judge just yet, hear me out. When Caroline first lived in San Diego, he would constantly go over to her house and visit with her and her father. He’s never had a happy home life and going over there was like a refuge for him. He was truly saddened when she moved away. Fast forward ten years later, she returns and finds Sebastian all grown up. She’s also starting to realize that he’s constantly flirting with her. But she’s married, albeit not happily, and he’s only seventeen. So what if he’s only four months shy of eighteen: It’s not right, right? However, Sebastian is relentless. He’s always finding ways to <i>hang out</i> with her. It’s only a matter of time when both succumb to their attraction. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Can you feel yourself inside me?”<br>His face was filled with amazement.<br>“Yes,” he whispered. “I can.”</i>
</b><br><br>Sebastian couldn’t believe she’d come back. He’s loved Caroline for a very long time. Crushing on her when he was only eight was just the starting point. Now that she’s here, he’s going to do everything he can to be with her. It’s always been Caroline. Always. They start an affair. Their first time was pretty memorable. Not only was Caroline Sebastian’s first, but this was also the time where she learns of his age. Heck yea, she freaked. She swore that she would wait til he turned eighteen before doing it again, but unfortunately, that plan blows up in her face. They seriously cannot resist each other. They enjoy being around each other, not only on a physical level, but also a very deep emotional level as well. Caroline starts to wake up. Sebastian makes her want things that she didn’t think were attainable. They set up a plan that when he turns 18, she will not only divorce David, but they plan on running away together. They have dreams of roaming Italy and starting a life together in New York. But how long can they keep their affair a secret?<br><br><b>
  <i>“I love you, Caroline. I always have. My whole life.”</i>
</b><br><br>The times when they were together were raw, beautiful and sensual. Sebastian is just the sweetest man in the world. He absolutely is 100%, head over heels, in love with Caroline. However, Caroline couldn’t help but constantly question their relationship. <i>Sebastian is gorgeous. Why does he even want me? Could they make their dream work?</i> Her fears were valid, but Sebastian kept reassuring her that they will <i>try</i> to do the best they can to be together. This book had me on pins and needles the whole time. I was waiting for the shoe to drop. I was emotionally invested in their relationship. When this story ended, I was a hot mess. I was glad I read this when I knew book two was out because as soon as I closed this book, I opened book two immediately. I LOVED THIS STORY!<br><br><i>*Photo provided by author</i><br></span>

<div id="review_786038911" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/786038911" />
    <a title="mich" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17575003-mich"><img alt="mich" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1361178507p2/17575003.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/786038911?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="mich" class="user" itemprop="url" name="mich" href="/user/show/17575003-mich">mich</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17575003-mich?shelf=will-read-next-one">will-read-next-one</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17575003-mich?shelf=good-new-to-me-author">good-new-to-me-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17575003-mich?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer786038911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9007755796641352139">Even if this had been the most well-written, touching book complete with hidden depths, I think you’d be hard pressed to stop your brain from screaming three things at you the entire time you’re reading it and that is: HE’S 17! and SHE’S MARRIED! and <i>HE’S 17!!!!!</i><br/><br/>The writing <i>is</i> good - it hooked me in right away just from the first few pages where we are introduced to Caroline, a woman who is caught in a loveless, unhappy marriage to a cold and selfish man. The author captured Caroline’s silent, a</span>
  <span id="freeText9007755796641352139" style="display:none">Even if this had been the most well-written, touching book complete with hidden depths, I think you’d be hard pressed to stop your brain from screaming three things at you the entire time you’re reading it and that is: HE’S 17! and SHE’S MARRIED! and <i>HE’S 17!!!!!</i><br /><br />The writing <i>is</i> good - it hooked me in right away just from the first few pages where we are introduced to Caroline, a woman who is caught in a loveless, unhappy marriage to a cold and selfish man. The author captured Caroline’s silent, accepting defeat of the life she found herself in to perfection - I found myself completely impressed with that. <br /><br />Caroline meets Sebastian early on in the book and folks, it was fricken uncomfortable as hell. Well, it was for me anyway. Uncomfortable, but also intriguing. And the author has balls too in not making Sebastian some kind of worldly, older than his actual age character. She doesn't try to trick us by making him seem mature for his age so that the whole affair feels just a little less taboo. Nope, dude is 17 and he acts like he’s 17 and he talks like he’s 17 (actually, he seemed even younger than that to me at times). Caroline is 30 and while she sometimes sounded her age, her immaturity in many scenes was a bit hard to swallow and had me thinking, who’s the fucking adult here anyway?!<br /><br />There were sex scenes aplenty and I think it was too much. The author really plays up the ‘close calls’ and ‘is <i>this</i> when they get caught?’ moments, and while it did create good tension and keep me on the edge of my seat at first, I slowly got annoyed at the frequency of the same damn things happening over and over. <br /><br />But the ending definitely delivers, it is dramatic and crazy and I loved it. Huge cliffhanger though, I need to read the next book right away. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I am absolutely giddy to see the reunion of Caro and Seb. I love LOVE a good reunion scene, and I hope theirs will not disappoint! I'm also happy to see from the blurb that it's 10 years later and we can see how things will play out between the two now (hopefully) mature adults.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9007755796641352139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_522099366" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/522099366" />
    <a title="R.E. Hunter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19358067-r-e-hunter"><img alt="R.E. Hunter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470168750p2/19358067.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/522099366?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="R.E. Hunter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="R.E. Hunter" href="/user/show/19358067-r-e-hunter">R.E. Hunter</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19358067-r-e-hunter?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19358067-r-e-hunter?shelf=arcs-galleys-requests-tours">arcs-galleys-requests-tours</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522099366" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8658730451826873641"><a href='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-N9Cxkmbn3Gw/UQyYAwiW6MI/AAAAAAAAAwA/21EyNTxXhxg/s1600/ed.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407502i/795970.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Rules are for the obedience of fools and the guidance of wise men."</i>
</b><br/><br/> Just ... wow. This book completely blew me away and left me so raw. I didn't know what to expect from this book but it wasn't this. I am floored. It gripped me and wouldn't let me go. I couldn't put it down. Couldn't get away from it.<br/><br/><i>The Education of Sebastian</i> has been on my TBR since its release and I was seeing great things about it. Although part of me wanted to read it, I was hesitant because of Sebastian's age. The</span>
  <span id="freeText8658730451826873641" style="display:none"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-N9Cxkmbn3Gw/UQyYAwiW6MI/AAAAAAAAAwA/21EyNTxXhxg/s1600/ed.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407502i/795970.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"Rules are for the obedience of fools and the guidance of wise men."</i>
</b><br><br> Just ... wow. This book completely blew me away and left me so raw. I didn't know what to expect from this book but it wasn't this. I am floored. It gripped me and wouldn't let me go. I couldn't put it down. Couldn't get away from it.<br><br><i>The Education of Sebastian</i> has been on my TBR since its release and I was seeing great things about it. Although part of me wanted to read it, I was hesitant because of Sebastian's age. The idea of a 30-year-old woman carrying on a sexual relationship with a 17-year-old boy really made me uncomfortable. But sometimes the best books make you uncomfortable and break down all those walls and preconceptions that you have and leave you seeing things from a whole new perspective. <i>The Education of Sebastian</i> is definitely one of those books. I went into it skeptical, but I promised myself that I would keep an open mind and I'm glad I did. I completely adored this story on every level.<br><br><b>
  <i>"What do you think I've got here that I wouldn't give up in a heartbeat to be with you? There's nothing to keep me here: I'll go anywhere, do anything to be with you."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-N1whwQvQEq4/UQyen4IoBOI/AAAAAAAAAww/bg9WTt4ttAU/s1600/seb.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407502i/795971.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sebastian is probably one of the most lovable male characters I've come across. He was gorgeous inside and out, completely sincere, not afraid to be emotional ... and watching him grow into his manhood and become more assertive and dominant was amazing. I liked Caroline as well, but she did drive me crazy with how she behaved in their relationship. Then again, I understood it. To believe that a 17-year-old boy could understand love and commitment is just impossible to comprehend but, at times, I think Seb understood it better than Caro ever could.<br><br><em>
  <strong>"It's always been you, Caro ... It's only ever been you."</strong>
</em><br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SEOlxMLhAMU/UQyet909vHI/AAAAAAAAAw4/HwbDmV4Lw8s/s1600/possible+caro.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407502i/795972.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The way these characters grow together, learn about each other and work through their relationship is beautiful. Their love is just <b>so big</b>. There is a ridiculous amount of sexual tension and the sex scenes in this book are intimate, honest, inviting and just plain sexy. I couldn't get enough of Caro and Seb. His boyish charm, his enthusiasm and how hard he loved Caroline just completely took me by surprise. I was swooning all over myself. He is definitely one of my new favorite book boyfriends. And I loved how Caroline found herself and her happiness and grew stronger because of their love.<br><br>Although I went into it uncomfortable and unsure, by the end of this book I was completely convinced. I wasn't seeing Sebastian as a child at all and I was rooting for he and Caroline all the way. I loved how Jane Harvey-Berrick wrote this story. I felt every single emotion she conveyed and was completely swept away by the story. The ending completely broke my heart in two and left me so raw and hurt. I don't want to give too much away, so all I can say is you just have to read this book and experience it for yourself. It was amazing.<br><br><i>Thank you so much Jane Harvey-Berrick for providing a review copy of this title, I cannot wait to jump right in to The Education of Caroline</i>!<br><br>More reviews at <a href="http://thebooklistreviews.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book List Reviews</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8658730451826873641" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="LZ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3702516-lz"><img alt="LZ" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/456470670?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="LZ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="LZ" href="/user/show/3702516-lz">LZ</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3702516-lz?shelf=books">books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer456470670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer906576398009391707"><b>This is for my fellow buddy readers!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397724i/767671._SY540_.jpg' width='320' height='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Whoa!! That ending, this book and these characters just blew me away! This book has been lurking in my TBR for quiet sometime and I'm so happy that I finally picked it up! I wasn't sure if I could get into the age difference between Caroline and Sebastian, but it was a non-issue. Their story was so well written and fleshed out that I just got lost in it. Slowly, I fell for Sebastian right along with Caroline. My heart was sad for the marriage she found herself</span>
  <span id="freeText906576398009391707" style="display:none"><b>This is for my fellow buddy readers!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397724i/767671._SY540_.jpg" width="320" height="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Whoa!! That ending, this book and these characters just blew me away! This book has been lurking in my TBR for quiet sometime and I'm so happy that I finally picked it up! I wasn't sure if I could get into the age difference between Caroline and Sebastian, but it was a non-issue. Their story was so well written and fleshed out that I just got lost in it. Slowly, I fell for Sebastian right along with Caroline. My heart was sad for the marriage she found herself in and I sympathized with her when she struggled to find herself amongst all of the new emotions.<br><br><b>"I knew I was wrong: I knew I was right."</b><br><br> And Sebastian, oh sweet Sebastian.....I just want to hold him!!! He has such a great mixture of vulnerability and strength. The abuse and negligence of his family resulted in an intensity that made him more mature than his age. He does have an air of innocence, but it doesn't feel creepy; actually, it made him more swoon worthy because his feelings are so raw. <br><br><b>"Your anything," he said seriously. "But I want to be your everything."</b><br><br>It was interesting to peak into the subculture of military life. The collection of characters in this book had me questioning humanity and common decency. There were quite a few instances I wanted to physically lash out, but there's also a lot of sweetness. As for that ending? Well, talk about going out with a bang! I'm anxiously waiting for the rest of this story. <br><br>Ok, I can't resist another for the road......<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397724i/767672._SY540_.png" width="300" height="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_532478419" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/532478419" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/532478419?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532478419" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1140632992509000853"><br/>This story follows Caroline Wilson – thirty years old, married eleven years, and trapped in a cold, loveless marriage. When she was seventeen, she was swept off her feet by David, a military surgeon. Dazzled by the sophisticated man, and ready to escape her mother's constant scrutiny, she made a rash decision and married David at nineteen. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“He hated the way I dressed, the way I spoke, what I spoke about and the things that interested me to speak about… He wasn’t always an unkind man… we were </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText1140632992509000853" style="display:none"><br />This story follows Caroline Wilson – thirty years old, married eleven years, and trapped in a cold, loveless marriage. When she was seventeen, she was swept off her feet by David, a military surgeon. Dazzled by the sophisticated man, and ready to escape her mother's constant scrutiny, she made a rash decision and married David at nineteen. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“He hated the way I dressed, the way I spoke, what I spoke about and the things that interested me to speak about… He wasn’t always an unkind man… we were just fundamentally unsuited to each other.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Because David is in the military, they had to move around a lot. In the beginning of the story, Caroline and David have just been relocated to San Diego, where Caroline first meets Sebastian. She is nineteen and he is eight. When she meets Sebastian's parents, she is horrified by the way they treat their son. Caroline felt bad for Sebastian and ends up forming a close friendship with the boy. Unfortunately, eventually Caroline and David are relocated to another base and she's forced to say goodbye to Sebastian. <br /><br />Nine years later, David and Caroline are relocated back to San Diego. While on the beach one day, Caroline meets Sebastian again. Caroline is now thirty and Sebastian is seventeen – all grown up, handsome, fit, and very charming. And Caroline soon learns Sebastian has been carrying a torch for Caroline since he was a boy. She resists his advances at first – determined to stay away from Sebastian and his good looks and charm. But there is an attraction there she can't resist. A feeling she has never felt for David. She feels alive with Sebastian. Figuring he was at least eighteen, she decides to give in to her feelings. <br /><br />But, when she finds out she actually had sex with a seventeen year old, she freaks out. She tells Sebastian there is no way they should ever be together again. Sebastian is determined to keep Caroline, so he talks her into a relationship without sex until he is of age. And because they both are extremely drawn to one another, she gives in. The chemistry between Sebastian and Caroline is incredibly intense and soon they find themselves in a very hot and heavy love affair. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“You are my world, Caro,” he said. “And you're mine.”</b>
</i> <br /><br />Because I am a woman in my mid-thirties, the thought of having sex with a seventeen year old man does nothing for me. I actually shiver at the thought. But the way Jane Harvel-Berrick writes Sebastian's character, I could understand Caroline's attraction towards him. He never had the parental nurturing and supervision most children have growing up. He's been taking care of himself since he was eight. With a drunk for a mother and an abusive father, Sebastian was forced to grow up fast. He's a mature, gorgeous, outgoing, kind man – not a boy. And because Caroline has been living in a stifling marriage for so long, she craved love, touch, kindness. She craved feeling alive again. Sebastian not only awoken her, but he made her feel special and beautiful. Not a servant to his needs like her husband. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Be happy, Caro, because that's what you deserve.<br />I love you, I have always loved you, and where I go after this world, I will always love you. <br />Sempre e per sempre.</i>
</b><br /><br />I fell hard for Sebastian right from the beginning. His deep love and affection for Caroline blew me away. The way he cared for Caroline and protected her made him swoon-worthy in my book. He definitely received a <i>very thorough</i> education from Caroline in the bedroom. The man's stamina is incredible. Phew. There were times when his alpha personality would come to the surface and it made me wonder what kind of man he would become as he aged. And I definitely plan to find out in the second book.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“There's nothing to forgive,” he said, his voice forceful. <br />“We feel in love: it's not a crime.”</i>
</b><br /><br />This is a well-written, lovely, and sensual book. This forbidden love story never came across as creepy. Even though Caroline was cheating on her husband the entire time, I never once felt bad about it because David was not a good husband. David may not be a completely cruel man, but he was insufferable, demeaning, demanding, and flat-out cold. He didn't treat Caroline with the kind of respect she deserved. And, let's face it, sometimes it is okay to step outside of the box and open your mind to reading different types of romance love stories. Even love stories that may be frowned upon by society. But, for Caroline and Sebastian, their love never felt wrong or uncomfortable. They have the kind of unconditional love that most people search for. Just because there is an awkward age difference, doesn't make it unnatural to love someone with so many years between them. <br /><br />I knew there was a cliffhanger when I began this book, but it didn't make it any easier when it ended. The ending emotionally wrecked me. I've never wanted a book to NOT end so bad in my life. But lucky the second book, <i>The Education of Caroline</i>, is out now! <br /><br />Rating:B+<br />Heat: Hot<br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>Arc kindly provided by the author.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1140632992509000853" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/541632951?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=older-woman-younger-man">older-woman-younger-man</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer541632951" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13802594059002032765"><b> 4.5 STARS</b><br/><br/>OMG!! What an ending!! I need to read the second book, Pronto!! Thank God I have it... PHEW!<br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>'Rules are for the obedience of fools and the guidance of wise men'</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410499i/804990._SX540_.jpg' width='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"There is nothing to forgive," he said, his voice forceful. "We fell in love. It's not a crime."</b>
</i><br/><br/>Caroline is 30 years old and in a loveless marriage to a US Navy Medical Officer. Sebastian is a 17 year old high school graduate, just four months away from 18. They met when Sebastian was just 8 years old and this is when he </span>
  <span id="freeText13802594059002032765" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 STARS</b><br><br>OMG!! What an ending!! I need to read the second book, Pronto!! Thank God I have it... PHEW!<br><br><br><b>
  <i>'Rules are for the obedience of fools and the guidance of wise men'</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410499i/804990._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"There is nothing to forgive," he said, his voice forceful. "We fell in love. It's not a crime."</b>
</i><br><br>Caroline is 30 years old and in a loveless marriage to a US Navy Medical Officer. Sebastian is a 17 year old high school graduate, just four months away from 18. They met when Sebastian was just 8 years old and this is when he started to fall in love with Caroline. But then her husband was relocated, and so Caroline leaves and doesn't return until 10 years later. In their first encounter, Caroline notices how handsome he's gotten and how eager Sebastian is to keep seeing her. She starts to feel uncomfortable at first, and tells him so, but then she couldn't help but feel attracted to him.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Why are you so scared? I mean, forget all that legal bullshit…why do you keep trying to…I don't know, make me change my mind? What do you think I've got here that I wouldn't give up in a heartbeat to be with you? There's nothing to keep me here. I'll go anywhere, do anything to be with you."</b>
</i><br><br>I wasn't sure initially, if the age difference was going to really put me off, due to Sebastian being underage and all. It ended up not bothering me too much in the end. I won't lie, some moments the age gap was more obvious then in others, and it was in those moments where I wasn't 100% okay with the relationship. I guess, I still would have liked for them to have waited until he was 18. Nevertheless, I really did enjoy the story.<br><br><i>
  <b>"I love you, Caroline. I always have. My whole life."<br><br>******<br><br>"Caro! Why are you crying?"<br>"Because I love you."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410499i/804991.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“What did I know of the kind of love that made it hard to breathe, where your body ached day and night for that connection with another, physically, mentally, spiritually? It was utterly new and terrifying and exhausting and wonderful. I was dazzled by the light that spilled from him into the shadow of my previous existence. He eclipsed everything, erased everything that had gone before. I was reborn – not just to him, but to myself. And I was ready for the adventure.”</b>
</i><br><br>Even though Caroline was 30, she at times seemed as innocent as Sebastian. I felt like she never really grew up and became her own person, because of the way she was treated by her husband. So in some ways, their behaviour was of a similar age. She was a doormat. David, her husband, demanded things be as he liked at all times. He never seemed to take an interest in, or encourage her to pursue what she was passionate about. He made her feel insignificant while he was always important. Everything they did was so mechanical and with no emotion. I don't know how she stood him for so long. I did feel very happy when she was able to finally leave that relationship and stand up for herself. Sebastian gave her that strength and support she needed to take that step. She was able to learn what real love felt like and also think about the possiblities to have in life. She finally felt alive and it was because of him.<br><br><b>
  <i>"You've given me back my self-esteem and you've given me hope for the future. You've given me love. You've given me yourself. There's nothing else I want."</i>
</b><br><br>Sebastian, sometimes, seemed to be mature for his young age. This was because he pretty much raised himself, since he practically had a nonexistent father and an alcoholic mother. That doesn't mean he didn't act like the teenager that he was, he definitely had his mood swings. He also was very sweet and so endearing. Almost everything that came out of his mouth had me absolutely MELTING! In the beginning, I thought, he couldn't possibly know what love is. I just thought he needed an out from his situation at home and latched himself on to Caroline. I soon realized that I was wrong. I believed him when he said he loved her. I adored him and just wanted him to have the happiness he deserved.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Caro, don't you understand how I feel about you? I love you, you're all I want. I want a future with you... I want our lives to be together. I'm not a kid, I've had to grow up fast. I've been taking care of myself for a long time now. And I want to take care of you."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445449938ra/16651921.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending was terrible!! Not that it was poorly written, but because of the events that took place. My heart was breaking and I hurt so badly for them. Why couldn't they just have waited for those four months to go by to start something! Then maybe it would have ended differently. It was a beautiful read and now I am DESPERATE to start the next!<br><br><i>
  <b>'Despite what happened that day, despite what happened later, I can't bring myself to regret the events of that summer, because Sebastian taught me how to love.'</b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13802594059002032765" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText6781009485130048686" style="display:none"> <b> 5+++ STARS, A MUST READ!!!!</b><br>I'll start off by saying there is no review I can write that will do this book justice. This is the love of story Caroline and Sebastian. The first they meet is when he is 8 and she's 21. Several years later they meet again when he's four months shy of his 18th birthday and Caroline is 30. When they meet again there is an instant connection that Caroline tries to fight because of their age difference and her marriage.<br><br>In the end their love was not to be denied and she gave in to their feelings. What followed is a powerful story of love, jealousy, infedelility, guilt, and passion. I was rooting for them the entire time as they were both so deserving of love. She, who is never shown any from her husband. <div id="review_524247297" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/524247297" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524247297?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=duet">duet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own-signed">pb-i-own-signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=sob-fest">sob-fest</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524247297" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12163911659147873543"><i>
  <b>“There’s nothing to forgive … We fell in love: it’s not a crime”</b>
</i><br/><br/>FUUUUUUUUUUUUUUCK!! I have been completely blown away by this book! Holy freaking intensity!<br/><br/>This is the story of a forbidden love story between a 30 year old married woman and a 17 year old boy. It possibly sounds a little gross, but I have to say, even if in my head I knew it was wrong, it didn’t feel wrong! It is an absolutely BEAUTIFUL love story, and I was completely swept away! <br/><br/>I fell in love with Sebastian right alongside </span>
  <span id="freeText12163911659147873543" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“There’s nothing to forgive … We fell in love: it’s not a crime”</b>
</i><br /><br />FUUUUUUUUUUUUUUCK!! I have been completely blown away by this book! Holy freaking intensity!<br /><br />This is the story of a forbidden love story between a 30 year old married woman and a 17 year old boy. It possibly sounds a little gross, but I have to say, even if in my head I knew it was wrong, it didn’t feel wrong! It is an absolutely BEAUTIFUL love story, and I was completely swept away! <br /><br />I fell in love with Sebastian right alongside Caroline. He is just incredible! He has endured so much in his life, he is mature, and seems so much older than 17. He knows what he wants, and what he wants is Caroline. <br /><br />Caroline is trapped in a loveless marriage where she is essentially a Stepford wife. Married at 19 to a Navy doctor who bullies and belittles her, she is lost, unhappy, and very much alone. When a lovestruck Sebastian enters her life with his heart in his hands, she starts to experience something that she has never felt before. <br /> <br /><i>“He had opened my eyes to a world of possibilities, to a world where I could be loved for myself.”</i><br /><br />And OH. MY. GOD!!! I was surprised at how quickly things progressed between the two of them, but it felt natural, and I loved seeing them together. There are some seriously hot and steamy scenes which had me fanning myself, and I loved the progression of things between them as they became used to each other, and as Sebastian grew more experienced. It was shown each time they were together, and I thought it was really well done. And equally as special is just watching them spend time together. Even though a lot of the time I had heart palpitations expecting them to get caught, the connection between them is strong, and the whole relationship is beautifully written.<br /><br />What I love about this book – it’s so real! The dialogue, the emotions, even the sex is all realistic. And I love that! I could empathise with everything that the characters go through. And even though at times I wanted to give Caroline a shake, I understood the reasoning behind her actions, and what she was feeling. Neither she or Sebastian are perfect, they both react emotionally to what is happening between them, and that is exactly how I would expect them to be as they both cave into the craziness and intensity of a love affair that will change both of their lives forever. <br /><br /><i>“You’ve taught me everything I know. … You’ve taught me who I can be, you’ve made me stronger. You make me want to see the magic in the world. I didn’t know falling in love could be…like this.”</i><br /><br />Even the side characters are well developed and realistic - their role in the story, as well as their reactions to the unfolding events round out the story beautifully. <br /><br />My heart was pounding through most of the story, and the angst level is off the charts! I kept waiting for the big ‘thing’ to happen. Seriously, I was a hot mess for most of the second half of the book! And when it happens – holy freaking clusterfuck! I could barely breathe! Massive, heartbreaking cliffy!!! So now, I’m wiping my tears, pulling up the big-girl panties, and diving straight into the next book!<br /><br /><i>“Here in this room, with our bodies entwined, I felt that I could trust this fierce love that had shattered and rebuilt my life. But outside, the world was a cold and dangerous place. I didn’t know if love would be enough.”</i><br /><br />I absolutely loved it - 5 stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12163911659147873543" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17307974717970235773"><br/><br/> Oh I can not believe they ended it there. But I am so glad to see the story will be continuing!<br/><br/>I was recommended this book by a friend and am so glad she did so!<br/><br/>The Education Of Sebastian was a brilliant story about self discovery and love. <br/><br/>Carolina is a 30 year old woman in a very unhappy, loveless marriage with David.   <span id="freeText17307974717970235773" style="display:none"><br /><br /> Oh I can not believe they ended it there. But I am so glad to see the story will be continuing!<br /><br />I was recommended this book by a friend and am so glad she did so!<br /><br />The Education Of Sebastian was a brilliant story about self discovery and love. <br /><br />Carolina is a 30 year old woman in a very unhappy, loveless marriage with David. He is a horrible man who hasn't the time of day for her, unless it is to order her around like a slave. And not the sexy kind of slave either!<br />One summer they find themselves moving back to San Diego, a place they lived when Carolina was 21. Whilst at the beach she discovers a handsome young man coming towards her as if he knows her.. Little did she know she did. It was her 8 year old neighbour grown up into a young man!<br />What happens next is a passionate love affair between Sebastian and Carolina. It's full of heartache, love and lots of sex. <br />I thoroughly enjoyed this story and was rooting for Carolina and Sebastian the whole way though. They deserve their HAE. <br /><br />This is the first book in a series and I can't wait for the next one to come out!</span>

<div id="review_905451211" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/905451211" />
    <a title="Shell The Belle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle"><img alt="Shell The Belle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399759491p2/15880350.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/905451211?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shell The Belle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shell The Belle " href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle">Shell The Belle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer905451211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13285583766455463447"><b>FOUR SOLID “A SUMMER OF STOLEN HAPPINESS” STARS</b><br/><br/>This story was really lovely. I am in love with this couple, especially Sebastian. <br/><br/>The only reason I did not give this five stars was the ending and, well, because I didn’t like the initial way they met. As you know from the blurb, when Caroline and Sebastian embark or their love affair, he is seventeen and she is thirty. However, they first meet ten years earlier, when she is twenty and he is just eight. Don’t get me wrong here, there was no inklin</span>
  <span id="freeText13285583766455463447" style="display:none"><b>FOUR SOLID “A SUMMER OF STOLEN HAPPINESS” STARS</b><br><br>This story was really lovely. I am in love with this couple, especially Sebastian. <br><br>The only reason I did not give this five stars was the ending and, well, because I didn’t like the initial way they met. As you know from the blurb, when Caroline and Sebastian embark or their love affair, he is seventeen and she is thirty. However, they first meet ten years earlier, when she is twenty and he is just eight. Don’t get me wrong here, there was no inkling of anything at all then, but it just creeped me out that she knew him as <i>a boy</i> is all.<br><br>I <b>
  <i>can</i>
</b> understand the change though, the seventeen year old Sebastian would have looked like a different person than the eight year old version; just recently I bumped into an old friend; I used to spend a lot of time at her house, she had three sons. When I last saw the youngest, George, he was around twelve years old, and when I saw him recently, he was twenty three!! And he in NO WAY resembled his blonde 12 year old self from back then; his hair was much darker, he was incredibly tall, very muscled and <b>very good looking indeed.</b><br><br>So I can kind of get it.<br><br>But anyway, it didn’t detract too much from my enjoyment, as I said earlier, I can totally understand the difference ten years can make going from a child to an adult.<br><br><b>Sebastian</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=n1q804" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408034531i/10800044._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Back to the story. Whereas I don’t usually like stories with cheating, I can completely understand why Caroline cheated on her husband, David. She was stuck in a loveless marriage to a man who had never shown her any love or affection. Never made her feel good about herself. You get the picture. She married him, a Military surgeon, at eighteen and he was eleven years older than her. She was desperate to leave home, and her mothers dream husband for her daughter. Very soon after she realized it was a mistake, but she had nowhere or no-one to turn to – her mother’s opinion was she had made her bed etc. <br><br>They lived at various army bases and Caroline was to him merely someone to fulfill the position of wife and arrange dinner parties and the like in her husbands numerous attempts to elevate his position within the Military base society. She married him because her mother made him appear like the perfect man. She (Caroline) didn’t know any better. For years she put on a façade of at least being content, but as those years slipped by one by one, she gradually became aware that she could not carry on with this life for very much longer. <br><br>There are no real descriptions from Caroline about herself in this story, I don’t even know what colour or style hair she has, so Ive chosen how I think she would look, Jennifer Anniston at thirty is perfect.<br><br><b>Caro</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=rc6bn9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408034531i/10800045.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <b>
  <i>”I looked at the man who was my husband, for better or worse. Nothing. My emotional gauge was running on empty. It had been that way for a long time. Until Sebastian.”</i>
</b><br><br><br> <b>
  <i>"Had I reached a turning point in my life, or was this merely a blip on a long and bleak horizon? Was leaping from a failed relationship into a doomed on the most sensible action for a woman of thirty? Rationally, no. But the feel of Sebastian’s body against mine, inside mine; his sweetness, his gentleness".</i>
</b><br><br>Her husband was nasty and selfish and considering his age, his actions most of the time were downright childish. He would sulk constantly, one example is after coming home drunk, he has a hangover the next morning;<br><br><b>
  <i> “I served his breakfast; three pieces of bacon, two eggs, two pancakes, syrup on the side and coffee. “This plates cold” he said, “Cant you do anything right?”</i>
</b><br><br>Well I would have tipped the fucking plate of food over the c***ts head!!<br><br>His sulk from his hangover and cold plate lasted well into the evening, until he goes to bed;<br> <br> <b>
  <i>”David, I noticed, had deliberately balled up his clothes and flung them onto my side of the bed, knowing I’d have to get up early to press his pants – again”</i>
</b><br><br>Well, I would have faked a migraine the next morning so that he’d have to iron his fucking “pants” himself!!<br><br>Another example is when they are putting on a dinner party for David’s “important” friends. Caroline has been slaving, literally, in the kitchen all day, making a huge effort, whilst David (the c**t) has been playing poker on his study computer. <br><br> <b>
  <i>”Then I saw that the dress I’d laid out to wear tonight had slid off the bed. David would have had to step over it three or four times as he’d moved around the bedroom, but he’d left it in a crumpled heap”</i>
</b><br><br>Waaattt?? Why doesn’t she call him on this? I would have HAD to confront him, but then I suppose David would just be ever more difficult. I was screaming at her <b>JUST CHUFFING LEAVE ALREADY FFS!! NO ONE SHOULD PUT UP WITH THAT!!</b><br><br>David is condescending, not only to Caroline, but anyone else on the base who isn’t what he considers high enough rank to bother with. And he berates Caroline for spending time with the families of these personnel, as though it will reflect badly on him!!<br><br>What a complete fucking arsehole. <br><br>Some have said why did she wait so long to contemplate leaving? And indeed, she did wait too long. But this kind of thing happens – you can find yourself in a relationship that truly doesn’t have any real basis for a life long haul, but because everyone around you thinks your partner is great, or because it becomes comfortable, whatever, a hundred other reasons too, you stay in it. And life goes on as you go about your day-to-day routines of work, career, etc, and only when something happens to make you realize you are wasting your life do you take the chance and leave. <br><br>Some people spend needless years waiting for something or someone better to come along, and they are the biggest fools; <b>
  <i>if you ever find yourself in this situation, don’t sit around waiting for your Prince Charming to come along and sweep you off your feet – you are not a Disney Princess and that wont happen!!</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2ryr8dh" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408090958i/10805814.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But Caroline knows that leaving David and starting again is not going to be easy;<br><br><br> <b>
  <i>”If I left David, I was well aware I would have nothing, not even my reputation. I had never lived on my own, never lived on what I could earn, never lived without the say-so of someone else. The unknowingness was terrifying”</i>
</b><br><br>It’s this kind of learned reliance on another that stops a lot of people from making that scary move and leaving a bad relationship. <br><br>Sebastian was the catalyst that sped things up rather than the reason for Caroline’s disillusionment with her own life and situation. His adoration of Caroline and his overwhelming love for this woman was simply too hard to ignore and she gave in to her emotions. <br><br> <b>
  <i>”I felt beautiful for the first time in my life, safe and secure.<br>Loved.<br>Cherished.”</i>
</b><br><br>Everyone should feel like that in a relationship, surely? David had simply made Caroline feel the opposite; dumb, useless, and unattractive. Sebastian gave her soul new life;<br><br><b>
  <i> “I love you Caroline” He spoke softly but the words were clear, spoken without expectation and with little hope”</i>
</b><br><br> <b>
  <i>”My mind filled with images of our sweet, gentle, glorious love making. I’d never been touched like that before – it had been an education, a delicious, dangerous awakening”</i>
</b><br><br> <b>
  <i>”A Summer of stolen happiness”</i>
</b><br><br>One thing I do not understand, and for love of God everyone reading this take note; Caroline said this;<br><br> <b>
  <i>"David had his salary paid into a savings account, and he gave me $1000 a month for groceries, gas for my car and utility bills. It was only just enough. I had no money of my own. When I’d had my job back east, David had insisted that my wages went into the communal pts, as he called it. Although I never saw the money again. I didn’t even know how much was in our savings account. What a humiliating admission.”</i>
</b><br><br>This made me so very angry when I read that. <br><b>Now look, if she is earning this money she has an absolute unequivocal right to ask:<br><br>a)	Where is this money going? <br>b)	 If it is going to a savings account, is it in joint names? Because it should be, she earned it too ffs!!<br>c)	HOW MUCH IS IN THE DAMN SAVINGS ACCOUNT???!!! Half of that is yours, Lady!! Claim it!!</b><br><br>But Caroline doesn’t question this, and she bloody well should!! Her husband is no doubt an ungrateful bully and Caroline has always done as she should, and never questioned. <br><br><b>Until Sebastian</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=ddke21" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408034531i/10800046.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She realises, at last, that she has to leave David; not simply because of Sebastian, but because this life with David is dead in the water and she wants out. She wants a life worth living and enjoying whilst she is still young enough to carve one out for herself. So, she finally starts to make plans to leave.<br><br> <b>
  <i>”I knew my marriage was over: it had been over for a long time before I’d met Sebastian, I’d just been too much of a coward to admit it”</i>
</b><br><br>What Caroline doesn’t realise is that when she first starts her affair with Sebastian, he is not eighteen, as she had thought, but seventeen, with four months until his birthday!! This adds extra complications because the law in state they are living in, California, has a legal age for sexual consent of eighteen. <br><br>Despite all her efforts to keep Sebastian at arms length when she realizes this, they are destined to be lovers sooner rather than later and are unable to stop the love and desire that threatens to consume them both. <br><br>They need to be really careful about being found out, though, as it could have serious consequences for Caroline, but hell if they don’t take the most logic defying risks and I was constantly terrified they were going to be seen/caught. All the way through I was like:<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=w1zecl" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408034531ra/10800047.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That seriously bothered me; I mean, if you are potentially looking at being prosecuted for this would you not take extra care? I mean EXTRA care?? <br><br>What I really did like though, was that although Caroline was making plans to leave David, she never once counted on Sebastian being the ultimate goal; she recognised that he was incredibly young and in no way expected any kind of commitment from him, in fact it was quite the opposite. She would tell him over and over that he had to be aware of the age difference, and that she was really was, in the grand scheme of things, too old for him. <br><br>She talked about him having children several years down the line, and that he really ought to be with someone closer his own age to make this more of a reality. So, although Caroline desperately wanted to be with Sebastian, as her love for him grew so did her desire to do the right thing by him and not allow him to be tied to her. She believed that their relationship had a “shelf life”, if you like, and what she feared most was that ten years later, Sebastian’s interest in her would wane and his head would be turned by younger women, thus leaving her forty years old and having to start again. <br><br>This thought plagued her throughout, and although her immediate plans were to leave California with Sebastian and live with him awhile in New York, this was mainly because she was determined also to get Sebastian away from his horrendous parents, and that way he would have a decent chance of making something of himself without the burden of his dreadful parents and wanted to help him get as far away from their grasp as possible.<br>In her mind, Carline believed that after several months to a year in New York, she and Sebastian would most likely then go their separate ways, leaving them both to carve out a life that they both were happy with.<br><br>However Sebastian thinks very differently; the only future he can see is with Caro;<br><br> <b>
  <i>”None of that matters, Caro. You’re wrong – I can’t imagine not wanting you, not ever, and not just physically. I enjoy being with you always. Forget all the legal bullshit – why do you keep trying to make me change my mind? What do you think I have here that I wouldn’t give up in a heartbeat to be with you? There’s nothing here for me, I’ll go anywhere, do anything to be with you”</i>
</b><br><br>And . . .<br><br> <b>
  <i>”If I was twenty five, and you were thirty eight, would we still be having this conversation? No.”</i>
</b><br><br> <b>
  <i>”I thought I was setting him free, but he saw it as my refusal to take a chance . . .on him, on us, on love – maybe even on myself”</i>
</b><br><br>Until finally . . .<br><br> <b>
  <i>”I didn’t have any words of opposition or defiance left in me. The future was unwritten: maybe one day I would be told for him and he would leave me – it seemed inevitable. But wouldn’t two or three years of love be worth having, regardless?”</i>
</b><br><br>I didn’t find the love affair hard to read, some have said because of Sebastian’s age it made it a little cringey for them. Not to me. The age of sexual consent in Britain is 16, so Sebastian was already a year passed that so I can get my head around it. And also to me, Sebastian was in some ways much older than his years. He had suffered physical, mental and verbal abuse at the hands of his parents, and has had to man up pretty quickly. He has pretty much been taking care of himself for years. In fact, at times, he seems to be more adult than Caroline. <br><br>By contrast, Caroline has led a very limited life with David. All she has really done is fetch and carry, cook and clean for him. Sex with David was vanilla, usually awkward and clumsy and simply for his gratification, and once that was achieved, rather quickly, that was it. Caroline is very naïve and is only now, at thirty, experiencing that stomach-flipping, butterflies in tummy sensation of falling in love. Sebastian shows her such tenderness and makes her feel things she has never felt about herself: Beauty and courage; and so she finally looks outside the box that is her marriage and builds on her confidence in her own abilities and self worth to be able to follow her own path without having to depend on anyone else to do so. This was already beginning to happen, but like I said, being with Sebastian helped it happen quicker than it was doing.<br><br><b>And you know what, sometimes life, or fate – whatever you choose to label it, sometimes it plays games; nasty cruel games. Sebastian and Caro where soulmates, destined to fall in love and truly belonged together. But life separated them by twelve fucking years – and not only that, threw them another curve ball and made Caro the older one.</b> <br><br> <b>
  <i>”We wandered along the cold, flat sand, under the moonlight, leaving the footprints of lovers”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=n5h1dl" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409474280i/10983786._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=142ag7r" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408034531i/10800048.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>The sex scenes;</b> <br><br>Well, some have said they were a bit too much, or icky, or too much information. Too realistic was one complaint. For me it was the realism that made it more sweet. The book is called “The Education Of Sebastian” for a reason – and his sexual ineptness, particularly at the very beginning of the affair was meant to be portrayed that way; it was meant to show his inexperience and how they both progressed as their relationship did – after all, Caroline wasn’t some older seductress who was sexually promiscuous, she was in many ways as clueless as Sebastian, and in reality, they taught each other many things over those three/four months. <br><br> <b>
  <i>”You’ve bought me to life, Sebastian, and you’ll never know how much I owe you because of that”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=nysqrm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408034531ra/10800049.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The writing is so beautiful. Having read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18929979.Lifers" title="Lifers by Jane Harvey-Berrick" rel="nofollow noopener">Lifers</a> by the same Author, although I didn’t really enjoy that one too much as it was a bit slow paced, I recognised the brilliance in Jane Harvey-Berrick and decided to give this Author another go. She didn’t disappoint. Berwick has the knack of writing in such a way that draws you into every page and holds you right there in the moment. It is so easy to read and makes everything seem incredibly real.<br><br><b>The Ending</b><br><br>Well, the ending just about floored me. Although it in no way surprised me!! It’s not how I wanted it to end, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I wanted them to both leave their present lives behind, move to New York together, spend that year together, and then, Sebastian’s education with Caroline complete, as Caroline predicted they both go their separate ways; Sebastian to complete his further studies and eventually meet someone who he can fall in love with, and Caroline to carve out her career in journalism that she wanted and then she to eventually meet someone with whom she too can fall in love with and build a lasting relationship. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>However, it is what it is, and I can’t wait for book two. <br><br> <b>
  <i>”I will never regret the events of that Summer, because Sebastian taught me how to love”</i>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
